House File 628 - Introduced


                                 HOUSE FILE 

                                 HOUSE FILE 
                                 HOUSE FILE                                  HOUSE FILE                                  BY  COMMITTEE ON WAYS AND
                                     MEANS

                                 (SUCCESSOR TO HSB 225)

 A BILL FOR

  1 An Act relating to Iowa's urban renewal law by modifying
  2    requirements for the annual report prepared by the
  3    legislative services agency, establishing restrictions on
  4    the use of divided revenues, modifying the methodology for
  5    calculating the amount of divided revenues, and including
  6    effective date provisions.
  7 BE IT ENACTED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 1171HV (1) 86
    md/sc

PAG LIN



  1  1    Section 1.  Section 331.403, subsection 3, paragraph d, Code
  1  2 2015, is amended to read as follows:
  1  3    d.  The legislative services agency, in consultation with
  1  4 the department of management, shall annually prepare a report
  1  5 for submission to the governor and the general assembly that
  1  6 summarizes and analyzes the information contained in the
  1  7 reports submitted under this subsection, section 357H.9,
  1  8 subsection 2, and section 384.22, subsection 2.                                      MEANS

  2 30    Sec. 4.    2 30    Sec. 4.    2 31 division of revenue limitations.
  2 32    1.  Each municipality having an urban renewal area in
  2 33 existence on the effective date of this Act that is subject to
  2 34 a division of revenue under section 403.19 that is not limited
  2 35 in duration under either section 403.17, subsection 10, or
  3  1 section 403.22, subsection 5, shall be subject to the assessed
  3  2 value adjustment in subsection 2.
  3  3    2.  a.  For each such urban renewal area described in
  3  4 subsection 1, the urban renewal area, including all applicable
  3  5 urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances providing
  3  6 for a division of revenue, shall continue in effect under
  3  7 this chapter, until such time that the urban renewal area
  3  8 is dissolved by the municipality or until the urban renewal
  3  9 area terminates under the conditions of this section. The
  3 10 municipality may continue to incur or issue additional costs
  3 11 or indebtedness for such urban renewal area, including loans,
  3 12 advances, and bonds, that qualify for payment from the special
  3 13 fund created in section 403.19 on or after the effective date
  3 14 of this Act and until dissolution or termination of the urban
  3 15 renewal area.
  3 16    b.  Notwithstanding any provision of this chapter to the
  3 17 contrary, for fiscal years beginning on or after July 1, 2016,
  3 18 when calculating a division of revenue for an urban renewal
  3 19 area described in subsection 1 for which the difference between
  3 20 the year of the assessment roll referred to in section 403.19,
  3 21 subsection 1, and the year of the assessment roll used to
  3 22 calculate the total amount of property taxes in the urban
  3 23 renewal area for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due
  3 24 and payable, exceeds twenty years, the assessed value of the
  3 25 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  3 26 the amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection 1, shall
  3 27 be increased by an amount equal to seven and one=half percent
  3 28 of the assessed value of the taxable property used to calculate
  3 29 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  3 30 for the fiscal year in which taxes are due and payable.
  3 31 Following the initial adjustment under this paragraph, the
  3 32 assessed value of the taxable property used to calculate the
  3 33 amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection 1, shall
  3 34 be further increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an
  3 35 amount equal to seven and one=half percent of the assessed
  4  1 value of the taxable property in the urban renewal area used
  4  2 to calculate the total amount of property taxes in the urban
  4  3 renewal area for the fiscal year in which taxes are due and
  4  4 payable, until such time as operation of this paragraph "b"
  4  5 would cause the assessed value of the taxable property used to
  4  6 calculate the amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection
  4  7 1, to exceed the assessed value of the taxable property in
  4  8 the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount of
  4  9 property taxes in the urban renewal area for the fiscal year in
  4 10 which the taxes are due and payable, or the twentieth fiscal
  4 11 year following the fiscal year for which the first adjustment
  4 12 is made under this section, whichever is earlier, at which time
  4 13 the urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 14 plans, projects, and ordinances providing for a division of
  4 15 revenue, shall terminate and be of no further force and effect.
  4 16    3.  The department of management shall adopt rules pursuant
  4 17 to chapter 17A necessary to implement and administer this
  4 18 section.

  4 16    3.  The department of management shall adopt rules pursuant
  4 17 to chapter 17A necessary to implement and administer this
  4 18 section.
  4 19    Sec. 5.  Section 403.19, Code 2015, is amended by adding the
  4 20 following new subsection:
  4 21      3  4 subsection 1, the urban renewal area, including all applicable
  3  5 urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances providing
  3  6 for a division of revenue, shall continue in effect under
  3  7 this chapter, until such time that the urban renewal area
  3  8 is dissolved by the municipality or until the urban renewal
  3  9 area terminates under the conditions of this section. The
  3 10 municipality may continue to incur or issue additional costs
  3 11 or indebtedness for such urban renewal area, including loans,
  3 12 advances, and bonds, that qualify for payment from the special
  3 13 fund created in section 403.19 on or after the effective date
  3 14 of this Act and until dissolution or termination of the urban
  3 15 renewal area.
  3 16    b.  Notwithstanding any provision of this chapter to the
  3 17 contrary, for fiscal years beginning on or after July 1, 2016,
  3 18 when calculating a division of revenue for an urban renewal
  3 19 area described in subsection 1 for which the difference between
  3 20 the year of the assessment roll referred to in section 403.19,
  3 21 subsection 1, and the year of the assessment roll used to
  3 22 calculate the total amount of property taxes in the urban
  3 23 renewal area for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due
  3 24 and payable, exceeds twenty years, the assessed value of the
  3 25 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  3 26 the amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection 1, shall
  3 27 be increased by an amount equal to seven and one=half percent
  3 28 of the assessed value of the taxable property used to calculate
  3 29 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  3 30 for the fiscal year in which taxes are due and payable.
  3 31 Following the initial adjustment under this paragraph, the
  3 32 assessed value of the taxable property used to calculate the
  3 33 amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection 1, shall
  3 34 be further increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an
  3 35 amount equal to seven and one=half percent of the assessed
  4  1 value of the taxable property in the urban renewal area used
  4  2 to calculate the total amount of property taxes in the urban
  4  3 renewal area for the fiscal year in which taxes are due and
  4  4 payable, until such time as operation of this paragraph "b"
  4  5 would cause the assessed value of the taxable property used to
  4  6 calculate the amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection
  4  7 1, to exceed the assessed value of the taxable property in
  4  8 the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount of
  4  9 property taxes in the urban renewal area for the fiscal year in
  4 10 which the taxes are due and payable, or the twentieth fiscal
  4 11 year following the fiscal year for which the first adjustment
  4 12 is made under this section, whichever is earlier, at which time
  4 13 the urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 14 plans, projects, and ordinances providing for a division of
  4 15 revenue, shall terminate and be of no further force and effect.
  4 16    3.  The department of management shall adopt rules pursuant
  4 17 to chapter 17A necessary to implement and administer this
  4 18 section.

  3 30 for the fiscal year in which taxes are due and payable.
  3 31 Following the initial adjustment under this paragraph, the
  3 32 assessed value of the taxable property used to calculate the
  3 33 amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection 1, shall
  3 34 be further increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an
  3 35 amount equal to seven and one=half percent of the assessed
  4  1 value of the taxable property in the urban renewal area used
  4  2 to calculate the total amount of property taxes in the urban
  4  3 renewal area for the fiscal year in which taxes are due and
  4  4 payable, until such time as operation of this paragraph "b"
  4  5 would cause the assessed value of the taxable property used to
  4  6 calculate the amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection
  4  7 1, to exceed the assessed value of the taxable property in
  4  8 the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount of
  4  9 property taxes in the urban renewal area for the fiscal year in
  4 10 which the taxes are due and payable, or the twentieth fiscal
  4 11 year following the fiscal year for which the first adjustment
  4 12 is made under this section, whichever is earlier, at which time
  4 13 the urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 14 plans, projects, and ordinances providing for a division of
  4 15 revenue, shall terminate and be of no further force and effect.
  4 16    3.  The department of management shall adopt rules pursuant
  4 17 to chapter 17A necessary to implement and administer this
  4 18 section.

  4  4 payable, until such time as operation of this paragraph "b"
  4  5 would cause the assessed value of the taxable property used to
  4  6 calculate the amount of taxes under section 403.19, subsection
  4  7 1, to exceed the assessed value of the taxable property in
  4  8 the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount of
  4  9 property taxes in the urban renewal area for the fiscal year in
  4 10 which the taxes are due and payable, or the twentieth fiscal
  4 11 year following the fiscal year for which the first adjustment
  4 12 is made under this section, whichever is earlier, at which time
  4 13 the urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 14 plans, projects, and ordinances providing for a division of
  4 15 revenue, shall terminate and be of no further force and effect.
  4 16    3.  The department of management shall adopt rules pursuant
  4 17 to chapter 17A necessary to implement and administer this
  4 18 section.
  4 19    Sec. 5.  Section 403.19, Code 2015, is amended by adding the
  4 20 following new subsection:

  4 35    Sec. 6.  EFFECTIVE UPON ENACTMENT.  This Act, being deemed of
  5  1 immediate importance, takes effect upon enactment.
  5  2                           EXPLANATION
  5  3 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  5  4 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  5  5    This bill relates to Iowa's urban renewal law.
  5  6    The bill requires the annual report prepared by the
  5  7 legislative services agency, in consultation with the
  5  8 department of management, under Code section 331.403, to
  5  9 contain a list of each county, city, or rural improvement zone
  5 10 that filed an annual report for the most recently ended fiscal
  5 11 year and each such entity's reported amount of loans, advances,
  5 12 indebtedness, or bonds that remain unpaid at the close of the
  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  4 23 section that is adopted on or after the effective date of
  4 24 this Act, including an ordinance providing for a division
  4 25 of revenue for an economic development area under section
  4 26 403.17, subsection 10, shall be limited to twenty years from
  4 27 the calendar year following the calendar year in which the
  4 28 municipality first certifies to the county auditor the amount
  4 29 of any loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds that qualify for
  4 30 payment from the division of revenue provided in this section.
  4 31 The urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 32 plans, projects, and ordinances, shall terminate and be of
  4 33 no further force and effect following the twenty=year period
  4 34 provided in this subsection.
  4 35    Sec. 6.  EFFECTIVE UPON ENACTMENT.  This Act, being deemed of
  5  1 immediate importance, takes effect upon enactment.
  5  2                           EXPLANATION
  5  3 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  5  4 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  5  5    This bill relates to Iowa's urban renewal law.
  5  6    The bill requires the annual report prepared by the
  5  7 legislative services agency, in consultation with the
  5  8 department of management, under Code section 331.403, to
  5  9 contain a list of each county, city, or rural improvement zone
  5 10 that filed an annual report for the most recently ended fiscal
  5 11 year and each such entity's reported amount of loans, advances,
  5 12 indebtedness, or bonds that remain unpaid at the close of the
  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  4 24 this Act, including an ordinance providing for a division
  4 25 of revenue for an economic development area under section
  4 26 403.17, subsection 10, shall be limited to twenty years from
  4 27 the calendar year following the calendar year in which the
  4 28 municipality first certifies to the county auditor the amount
  4 29 of any loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds that qualify for
  4 30 payment from the division of revenue provided in this section.
  4 31 The urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 32 plans, projects, and ordinances, shall terminate and be of
  4 33 no further force and effect following the twenty=year period
  4 34 provided in this subsection.
  4 35    Sec. 6.  EFFECTIVE UPON ENACTMENT.  This Act, being deemed of
  5  1 immediate importance, takes effect upon enactment.

  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  4 29 of any loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds that qualify for
  4 30 payment from the division of revenue provided in this section.
  4 31 The urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 32 plans, projects, and ordinances, shall terminate and be of
  4 33 no further force and effect following the twenty=year period
  4 34 provided in this subsection.
  4 35    Sec. 6.  EFFECTIVE UPON ENACTMENT.  This Act, being deemed of
  5  1 immediate importance, takes effect upon enactment.
  5  2                           EXPLANATION
  5  3 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  5  4 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  5  5    This bill relates to Iowa's urban renewal law.
  5  6    The bill requires the annual report prepared by the
  5  7 legislative services agency, in consultation with the
  5  8 department of management, under Code section 331.403, to
  5  9 contain a list of each county, city, or rural improvement zone
  5 10 that filed an annual report for the most recently ended fiscal
  5 11 year and each such entity's reported amount of loans, advances,
  5 12 indebtedness, or bonds that remain unpaid at the close of the
  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  4 30 payment from the division of revenue provided in this section.
  4 31 The urban renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal
  4 32 plans, projects, and ordinances, shall terminate and be of
  4 33 no further force and effect following the twenty=year period
  4 34 provided in this subsection.

  5 12 indebtedness, or bonds that remain unpaid at the close of the
  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  4 35    Sec. 6.  EFFECTIVE UPON ENACTMENT.  This Act, being deemed of
  5  1 immediate importance, takes effect upon enactment.
  5  2                           EXPLANATION
  5  3 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  5  4 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  5  5    This bill relates to Iowa's urban renewal law.
  5  6    The bill requires the annual report prepared by the
  5  7 legislative services agency, in consultation with the
  5  8 department of management, under Code section 331.403, to
  5  9 contain a list of each county, city, or rural improvement zone
  5 10 that filed an annual report for the most recently ended fiscal
  5 11 year and each such entity's reported amount of loans, advances,
  5 12 indebtedness, or bonds that remain unpaid at the close of the
  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.

  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  5  6    The bill requires the annual report prepared by the
  5  7 legislative services agency, in consultation with the
  5  8 department of management, under Code section 331.403, to
  5  9 contain a list of each county, city, or rural improvement zone
  5 10 that filed an annual report for the most recently ended fiscal
  5 11 year and each such entity's reported amount of loans, advances,
  5 12 indebtedness, or bonds that remain unpaid at the close of the
  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a

  5 13 fiscal year, and which qualify for payment from the special
  5 14 fund created in Code section 403.19, including interest
  5 15 negotiated on such loans, advances, indebtedness, or bonds.
  5 16    The bill provides that urban renewal plans and urban
  5 17 renewal projects approved on or after the effective date of
  5 18 the bill shall not include the use of revenue resulting from
  5 19 a division of taxes for a public building that is exempt
  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,
  5 21 equipment, remodeling, maintenance, repair, or reconstruction
  5 22 of, and additions or extensions to, such a building. The bill
  5 23 also modifies provisions governing the use of such revenues
  5 24 for public buildings for plans and projects approved before
  5 25 the effective date of the bill to include the maintenance and
  5 26 repair of such public buildings.
  5 27    New Code section 403.18A provides that each municipality
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.

  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86

  5 20 from taxation, including the grounds of, and the erection,

  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.
       LSB 1171HV (1) 86
       md/sc
  5 28 having an urban renewal area in existence on the effective
  5 29 date of the bill that is subject to a division of revenue that
  5 30 is not limited in duration under either Code section 403.17,
  5 31 subsection 10 (20 years) or Code section 403.22, subsection 5
  5 32 (10 years) shall be subject to the assessed value adjustment
  5 33 provided for in the bill.  Under the bill, when calculating a
  5 34 division of revenue for such an urban renewal area for a fiscal
  5 35 year beginning on or after July 1, 2016, and for which the
  6  1 difference between the year of the assessment roll referred
  6  2 to in Code section 403.19, subsection 1, (establishing a base
  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
  6 30 no further force and effect.
  6 31    The bill provides that except for certain divisions of
  6 32 revenue authorized for certain housing and residential
  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,

  6 33 development under Code section 403.22, an ordinance providing
  6 34 for a division of revenue under Code section 403.19 that is
  6 35 adopted on or after the effective date of the bill shall be
  7  1 limited to 20 years from the calendar year following the
  7  2 calendar year in which the municipality first certifies to the
  7  3 county auditor the amount of any loans, advances, indebtedness,
  7  4 or bonds which qualify for payment from the division of revenue
  7  5 provided in Code section 403.19. Under the bill, the urban
  7  6 renewal area, including all applicable urban renewal plans,
  7  7 projects, and ordinances shall terminate and be of no further
  7  8 force and effect following the 20=year period provided in the
  7  9 bill.
  7 10    The bill takes effect upon enactment.

  6  3 assessed value), and the year of the assessment roll used
  6  4 to calculate the total amount of property taxes under Code
  6  5 section 403.19 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are
  6  6 due and payable, exceeds 20 years, the assessed value of the
  6  7 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6  8 the amount of taxes under Code section 403.19, subsection 1,
  6  9 shall be increased by an amount equal to 7.5 percent of the
  6 10 assessed value used to calculate the total amount of property
  6 11 taxes in the urban renewal area for the applicable fiscal
  6 12 year. Following the initial adjustment, the assessed value
  6 13 of the taxable property used to calculate the amount of taxes
  6 14 under Code section 403.19, subsection 1, shall be further
  6 15 increased for each subsequent fiscal year by an amount equal
  6 16 to 7.5 percent of the assessed value of the taxable property
  6 17 in the urban renewal area used to calculate the total amount
  6 18 of property taxes for the applicable fiscal year, until
  6 19 by operation of the bill the assessed value of the taxable
  6 20 property used to calculate the amount of taxes under Code
  6 21 section 403.19, subsection 1, exceeds the assessed value of the
  6 22 taxable property in the urban renewal area used to calculate
  6 23 the total amount of property taxes in the urban renewal area
  6 24 for the fiscal year in which the taxes are due and payable, or
  6 25 the twentieth fiscal year following the fiscal year for which
  6 26 the first adjustment is made under this section, whichever
  6 27 is earlier, at which time the urban renewal area, including
  6 28 all applicable urban renewal plans, projects, and ordinances
  6 29 providing for a division of revenue, shall terminate and be of
